							holding_type = tribal
						}
					}
				}
			}
			trigger_else_if = {
				limit = {
					attacker = {
						is_nomadic = no
						is_tribal = no
					}

					defender = {
						is_nomadic = yes
					}

				}

				any_direct_de_jure_vassal_title = {
					any_direct_de_jure_vassal_title = {
						OR = {
							holding_type = castle
							holding_type = city
						}
					}
				}
			}

			trigger_if = {
				limit = {
					attacker = {
						has_character_flag = is_temujin
						has_landed_title = e_mongol_empire
						demesne_size >= 1
					}
				}

				defender = {
					NOT = { has_landed_title = e_china_west_governor }
				}
			}
		}

		coronation_factor = yes

		# TODO: Review these
		# Try to guide the Hordes in the right direction
		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 0.1

			attacker = {
				OR = {
					dynasty = 613 # Seljuks
					dynasty = 800 # Timurids

					primary_title = {
						title = e_il-khanate
					}
				}
			}

			OR = {
				empire = {
					NOR = {
						title = e_persia
						title = e_byzantium
						title = e_arabia
					}
				}

				defender = {
					primary_title = {
						title = e_golden_horde
					}

					year < 1300
				}

				# CK2Plus
				defender = {
					primary_title = { title = e_chagatai }
					year < 1300
				}
			}
		}

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 0.1

			attacker = {
				primary_title = {
					title = e_golden_horde
				}
			}

			OR = {
				empire = {
					OR = {
						title = e_persia
						title = e_byzantium
						title = e_arabia
					}
				}

				defender = {
					primary_title = {
						title = e_il-khanate
					}

					year < 1300
				}
			}
		}

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 0.1

			attacker = {
				culture = hungarian

				primary_title = {
					OR = {
						title = k_hungary
						title = e_carpathia
					}
				}
			}

			empire = {
				OR = {
					title = e_tartaria
					title = e_russia
				}
			}
		}

		# CK2Plus
		mult_modifier = { #Prefer bigger targets
			factor = 1.5
			attacker = {
				tier = KING
			}
		}
		mult_modifier = { #Prefer bigger targets
			factor = 2.0
			attacker = {
				tier = EMPEROR
			}
		}
		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			attacker = {
				OR = {
					dynasty = 613 # Seljuks
					dynasty = 800 # Timurids
					primary_title = { title = e_il-khanate }
					trigger_if = {
						limit = {
							NOT = {
								any_realm_province = { region = custom_persia }
							}
						}
						primary_title = { title = e_mongol_empire }
					}
				}
			}
			capital_scope = { region = custom_persia }
		}
		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			attacker = {
				primary_title = { title = e_golden_horde }
			}
			capital_scope = {
				OR = {
					region = custom_cuman
					region = custom_perm
					region = custom_volga
				}
			}
		}
		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			attacker = {
				primary_title = { title = e_mongol_empire }
				NOT = { any_realm_province = { region = custom_cuman } }
			}
			capital_scope = { region = custom_cuman }

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			attacker = { primary_title = { title = e_mongol_empire } }
			capital_scope = { region = custom_khwarizm }

		mult_modifier = {

			OR = {
				capital_scope = {
